## Conversation Summary
- **Documentation Creation**: Created comprehensive documentation for inventory management system improvements in Arabic, including 6 detailed markdown files covering improvement requirements, shared functions for general level, oils-greases warehouse, spare-parts warehouse, and development roadmap
- **Shared Services Implementation**: Created 5 shared service modules (InventoryItemsService, TransactionNumberService, StorageLocationsService, ExcelExportService, CategoryService) and 5 oils-greases transaction services (Purchase, Issue, Transfer, Return, Adjust)
- **TypeScript Compilation Fixes**: Fixed multiple TypeScript errors by correcting Prisma model names (adding INV_ prefix), field names (nameAr, purchaseNumber, issuanceNumber, etc.), and separating warehouse logic to avoid union type issues
- **Service Replacement**: Successfully replaced Purchase and Issue services in oils-greases handlers to use new shared services, reducing code by 40-70%
- **Testing**: Both Purchase and Issue operations tested successfully in production with real data

## Key Insights
- **Prisma Schema**: Database uses prefixed model names (INV_OilsGreasesItem, INV_SparePart, INV_OilsGreasesPurchase, INV_OilsGreasesIssuance, INV_StorageLocation, INV_OilsGreasesCategory) and specific field names (nameAr not name, purchaseNumber not transactionNumber, createdBy as BigInt)
- **TypeScript Union Types**: Cannot use dynamic model selection with union types; must use if/else branching for warehouse-specific logic to avoid TypeScript compilation errors
- **Code Reduction**: Shared services approach reduced code duplication by 40-70% while maintaining full functionality
- **Testing Success**: Purchase operation tested successfully (added 20 units to item, quantity changed from 50â†’70), Issue operation tested successfully (issued 10 units to employee and equipment, quantity changed from 70â†’60)
- **User Preference**: User wants to replace functions one-by-one and test each before proceeding to ensure correctness

```prisma
  toLocationId    Int

  createdBy       BigInt

}
```

```typescript
export class InsufficientStockError extends Error {
  constructor(
    public itemName: string,
    public available: number,
    public requested: number
  ) {
    super(`Insufficient stock for ${itemName}`)
  }
}

export class ItemNotFoundError extends Error {
  constructor(public itemId: number) {
    super(`Item ${itemId} not found`)
  }
}

// ÙÙŠ handlers

  await operation()
} catch (error) {

      `âŒ Ø§Ù„ÙƒÙ…ÙŠØ© ØºÙŠØ± ÙƒØ§ÙÙŠØ©\n\n`
```

### 5ï¸âƒ£ Caching Layer (Ø£ÙˆÙ„ÙˆÙŠØ© Ù…Ù†Ø®ÙØ¶Ø© ğŸŸ¢)

**Ù„Ù„ØªÙ‚Ø§Ø±ÙŠØ± ÙˆØ§Ù„Ø¥Ø­ØµØ§Ø¦ÙŠØ§Øª:**
```typescript
// src/modules/cache/cache.service.ts
export class CacheService {
  private static cache = new Map<string, { data: any; expiry: number }>()
  
  static async get<T>(key: string): Promise<T | null> {
    const cached = this.cache.get(key)
    if (cached && cached.expiry > Date.now()) {
      return cached.data
    }
    return null
  }
  
  static async set(key: string, data: any, ttl: number = 300000) {
    this.cache.set(key, { data, expiry: Date.now() + ttl })
  }
}

// ÙÙŠ ReportsService
const cacheKey = `inventory:summary:${warehouse}`
const cached = await CacheService.get(cacheKey)
if (cached) return cached

const summary = await this.calculateSummary(warehouse)
await CacheService.set(cacheKey, summary, 300000) // 5 Ø¯Ù‚Ø§Ø¦Ù‚
return summary
```

### 1ï¸âƒ£ **Jest + Supertest** (Ù…ÙˆØ¬ÙˆØ¯ ÙÙŠ Ø§Ù„Ù…Ø´Ø±ÙˆØ¹ âœ…)

**Ù„Ù„Ø§Ø®ØªØ¨Ø§Ø±Ø§Øª Ø§Ù„Ø¢Ù„ÙŠØ©:**

```typescript
// tests/integration/oils-greases/purchase.test.ts
import { Database } from '#root/modules/database/index.js'
import { OilsGreasesPurchaseService } from '#root/modules/services/inventory/oils-greases/purchase.service.js'

describe('Purchase Transaction', () => {
  beforeAll(async () => {
    await Database.connect()
  })

  afterAll(async () => {
    await Database.disconnect()
  })

  it('should create purchase and increase quantity', async () => {
    // Arrange
    const itemId = 1
    const initialItem = await Database.prisma.iNV_OilsGreasesItem.findUnique({
      where: { id: itemId }
    })
    const quantityToAdd = 50

    // Act
    await OilsGreasesPurchaseService.createPurchase({
      itemId,
      quantity: quantityToAdd,
      unitPrice: 100,
      supplierName: 'Test Supplier',
      userId: BigInt(123)
    })

    // Assert
    const updatedItem = await Database.prisma.iNV_OilsGreasesItem.findUnique({
      where: { id: itemId }
    })
    expect(updatedItem.quantity).toBe(initialItem.quantity + quantityToAdd)
  })

  it('should throw error for invalid quantity', async () => {
    await expect(
      OilsGreasesPurchaseService.createPurchase({
        itemId: 1,
        quantity: -10, // Ø³Ø§Ù„Ø¨
        unitPrice: 100,
        userId: BigInt(123)
      })
    ).rejects.toThrow()
  })
})
```

**ØªØ´ØºÙŠÙ„:**
```bash
npm test -- oils-greases/purchase
```

```javascript
import http from 'k6/http'
import { check, sleep } from 'k6'

export const options = {
  stages: [
    { duration: '30s', target: 20 }, // 20 Ù…Ø³ØªØ®Ø¯Ù…
    { duration: '1m', target: 50 },  // 50 Ù…Ø³ØªØ®Ø¯Ù…
    { duration: '30s', target: 0 },  // ØªÙ‚Ù„ÙŠÙ„ ØªØ¯Ø±ÙŠØ¬ÙŠ
  ],
}

export default function () {
  const res = http.post('http://localhost:3000/webhook', {
    update_id: 123,
    message: { text: '/start' }
  })
  
  check(res, {
    'status is 200': (r) => r.status === 200,
    'response time < 500ms': (r) => r.timings.duration < 500,
  })
  
  sleep(1)
}
```

### 6ï¸âƒ£ **Database Testing Tools**

**Prisma Studio + SQL Scripts:**

```sql
-- tests/sql/verify-purchase.sql
-- Ø§Ù„ØªØ­Ù‚Ù‚ Ù…Ù† ØµØ­Ø© Ø§Ù„Ø¨ÙŠØ§Ù†Ø§Øª Ø¨Ø¹Ø¯ Ø§Ù„Ø´Ø±Ø§Ø¡

SELECT 
  i.id,
  i.nameAr,
  i.quantity as current_quantity,
  p.quantity as purchased_quantity,
  p.unitPrice,
  p.totalAmount,
  p.createdAt
FROM INV_OilsGreasesItem i
JOIN INV_OilsGreasesPurchase p ON p.itemId = i.id
WHERE p.id = (SELECT MAX(id) FROM INV_OilsGreasesPurchase)
```
